class Solution {
    public long sumDigitDifferences(int[] nums) {
        Deque<Integer> deque = new ArrayDeque<>();
        for (int i : nums) {
            deque.add(i);
        }
        long result = 0;
        int n = nums.length;
        while (true) {
            boolean isBreak = false;
            int[] count = new int[10];
            for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
                if (nums[i] == 0) {
                    isBreak = true;
                    break;
                }
                count[nums[i] % 10]++;
                nums[i] /= 10;
            }
            int temp = n;
            for (int i : count) {
                if (i != 0) {
                    result += (temp - i) * i;
                }
                temp -= i;
            }
            if (isBreak)
            break;
        }
        return result;
    }
}
